<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7NH"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7NI">The land did not fall to the good man for another five years, and by that time Roland was a gunslinger, his father was dead, he himself had become a matricide—and the world had moved on.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7NJ"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7NK">The long years and long rides had begun.</span></p>
<div class="calibre_5" aid="BE7NL"> </div><h3 class="calibre_8" aid="BE7NM"><span class="calibre9" aid="BE7NN"><span class="bold1" aid="BE7NO">XIII</span></span></h3><div class="calibre_1" aid="BE7NP"> </div>
<p class="calibre_9" aid="BE7NQ"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7NR">“Look,” Jake said, pointing upward.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7NS"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7NT">The gunslinger looked up and felt a twinge in his right hip. He winced. They had been in the foothills two days now, and although the waterskins were almost empty again, it didn’t matter now. There would soon be all the water they could drink.</span></p>
<a aid="BE7NU"></a>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7NV"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7O0">He followed the vector of Jake’s finger upward, past the rise of the green plain to the naked and flashing cliffs and gorges above it . . . on up toward the snowcap itself.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7O1"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7O2">Faint and far, nothing but a tiny dot (it might have been one of those motes that dance perpetually in front of the eyes, except for its constancy), the gunslinger beheld the man in black, moving up the slopes with deadly progress, a miniscule fly on a huge granite wall.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7O3"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7O4">“Is that him?” Jake asked.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7O5"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7O6">The gunslinger looked at the depersonalized mote doing its faraway acrobatics, feeling nothing but a premonition of sorrow.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7O7"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7O8">“That’s him, Jake.”</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7O9"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OA">“Do you think we’ll catch him?”</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OB"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OC">“Not on this side. On the other. And not if we stand here talking about it.”</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OD"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OE">“They’re so high,” Jake said. “What’s on the other side?”</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OF"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OG">“I don’t know,” the gunslinger said. “I don’t think anybody does. Maybe they did once. Come on, boy.”</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OH"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OI">They began to move upward again, sending small runnels of pebbles and sand down toward the desert that washed away behind them in a flat bake-sheet that seemed to never end. Above them, far above, the man in black moved up and up and up. It was impossible to see if he looked back. He seemed to leap across impossible gulfs, to scale sheer faces. Once or twice he disappeared, but always they saw him again, until the violet curtain of dusk shut him from their view. When they made their camp for the evening, the boy spoke little, and the gunslinger wondered if the boy knew what he himself had already intuited. He thought of Cuthbert’s face, hot, dismayed, excited. He thought of the bread. He thought of the birds. It ends this way, he thought. Again and again it ends this way. There are quests and roads that lead ever onward, <a aid="BE7OJ"></a>and all of them end in the same place—upon the killing ground.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OK"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7OL">Except, perhaps, the road to the Tower. There ka might show its true face.</span></p>
<p class="calibre_10" aid="BE7OM"><span class="calibre3" aid="BE7ON">The boy, the sacrifice, his face innocent and very young in the light of their tiny fire, had fallen asleep over his beans. The gunslinger covered him with the horse blanket and then curled up to sleep himself.</span></p><p class="calibre10" aid="BE7OO"> </p>
<p class="calibre_" aid="BE7OP"><img alt="thegunsling_150_0.jpg" class="calibre13" src="kindle:embed:0006?mime=image/jpeg"/></p>
<a aid="BE7OQ"></a>
<div class="mbp_pagebreak" id="calibre_pb_21" aid="BE7OR"></div>
